  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5abceb75-fe3e-4852-ad01-a474e16e1fcc'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer9215982579100812580">The last few days have been the darkest of Sally’s life. After experiencing the joy of finding her mate, she now suffers the pain of losing everything she holds dear.   <span id="freeText9215982579100812580" style="display:none">The last few days have been the darkest of Sally’s life. After experiencing the joy of finding her mate, she now suffers the pain of losing everything she holds dear. Both the Romanian and Serbian packs have been captured, ripping Sally’s soul mate away from her almost as soon as she had found him. Her best friend and the emotional glue that usually holds Sally together, Jacque Pierce, lies writhing in a restless coma, having been put down by Desdemona’s dark magic. Jennifer Adams, the unshakable one, has revealed to her friends and her mate that she is pregnant, but the Fates have marked her unborn baby for death. Though she rails against the darkness, deep inside Jen knows that Decebel’s baby must die as payment for her own life, and the knowledge is tearing her soul to pieces. Cypher, King of the Warlocks, has claimed Jacque’s mother as his mate and agreed to help Desdemona open a door that would release a horde of demons from beyond the Veil. <br /> <br />Though her world is crashing down around her, Sally holds out hope. The Great Luna is not sitting idly by. She has commanded the Fey council to call upon the packs—all of them. And though Cypher looks for a way to open the Veil for Desdemona, he struggles to protect Lilly and the wolves at the same time. Peri, the ever-courageous High Fae, and a contingent of the remaining females of the Romanian and Serbian packs, push on through the rough Carpathian Mountains. Though they are bound to the human realm, they continue to search for a way to cross over to the land of the Fey. Meanwhile, in reluctant obedience to the Great Luna, the Fey council sends representatives to the far corners of the globe, meeting with the pack Alphas. The Fey must convince the Alphas of every pack to lay aside their petty territorial squabbles and battles of dominance. If they refuse, both the humans and the supernatural races will fall at Mona’s feet.<br /> <br />Sally holds to a shred of hope. Though Vasile, Decebel, and their pack mates endure the torture of the In-Between, living their worst nightmares over and over, Sally holds. Though she knows that it is only a matter of time before their wolves take over, she holds. Sally knows that if the males die, then so too will their mates who have performed the Blood Rites, including her best friends Jen and Jacque. Yet she holds. If the males lose themselves to their wolves and turn feral, so too do their mates. Still she holds. Though Vasile, the strongest Alpha in their history to unite the wolves, is lost beyond the Veil, Sally holds. Though Decebel, the only other wolf besides Vaile strong enough to unite the packs, suffers beyond the Veil, Sally will hold. No one is left to unite their race, and defeat Desdemona. Yet Sally still holds. She holds out hope that the Great Luna will not abandon them, cannot abandon them. Throughout the centuries, the Great Luna has always provided a gypsy healer to the packs, especially in times of great need. Now Sally is that healer. Sally fears what role she has to play in the defeat of Desdemona, but she will play it. Though heaven and hell unite against her, she WILL play it.<br /> <br />For too long the supernatural races have lived in separation, warring amongst themselves, allowing trivial power plays and selfish disputes to keep them from uniting. That separation has made them weak. Now, being summoned as a collective force to the same land, will they come? Will they come in numbers greater than have been seen in centuries? Will they destroy each other and save Mona the trouble, or will they finally unite and fight as one?</span>
  <a data-text-id="9215982579100812580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Honestly, you just have to feel it. You have to want to write, and it has to be something you can imagine. If you really can’t think of anything to wr<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Honestly, you just have to feel it. You have to want to write, and it has to be something you can imagine. If you really can’t think of anything to write, think of a story in your head. If you can’t imagine it, you won’t be able to write it <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

The three besties aren't who they were months ago. They have grown, grown into beauty and life....into love and their souls. I cried at the end. Like this. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380748913i/3119063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Well....not like that...I had a bloated nose and deformed eye bags after the breakdown but still....and all the poor mates and hubbys!! <br><br>Wat they have to suffer.   <span id="freeText1088111107464012639" style="display:none"><br>Quinn!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/458624.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I...I....I'm speechless and hurting a lot!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395050ra/760754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">This is going to be a very messy review because my emotions are out of control! By the way, this review has <u>spoilers</u>, so don't try to be curious if you don't want to know xD<br><br>Was it worth the waiting?<br>Of course it was! *freaking out* There must be anotheeeer.<br><br>What did you think about Sally?<br>I still don't love Sally, but she has been growing up a lot since the last book. Furthermore, I'm really happy she stopped using her "inner Jen" and started to be herself.<br><br>What did you think about Costin?<br>He surprised me! Costin in this book was <b>H O T</b> and his comments were hilarious. Most of the time when I was reading about him I was like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396430ra/764150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">He said and did so many cute and sassy things to his mate that I felt so envious of Sally for having such a man. I thought a lot of these characters -which I love- were going to die.<br><br>What happened to Desdemona (or whatever her name is)?<br>Desdemona was a <s>bitch</s> bad creature! Now there's another villain named Reyaz, and he seems more powerful than the <s>bitch</s> witch.<br><br><b>SUPER SPOILER ALERT AHEAD:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396430ra/764151.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jen and Dec?<br>I LOVE THEM! Jen and Dec are the kick-ass couple! They have overcome so much together since the third book. I feel like they have the strongest love of them all <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380748913ra/3119076.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> I wouldn't mind reading 3 more books just about them. <br><br>I'm worried how Decebel sacrificed himself, of course it was cute because he's already acting like a dad. Nevertheless, I hope there's a way to save him! If Jen and Dec cannot be together anymore my heart will literally break, and I would have to start calling to Azkaban so they can reserve a room for me <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380748913ra/3119077.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In conclusion, if you're going to read this book, make sure you have plenty of free time. You can also pick a supportive friend (thank God I had one, she was very patient with me although  I was freaking her out the whole time lol) so you can share your suffering without killing yourself xD  Also, make sure you don't have classes/work/family reunions etc etc because if you're like me, you will end up like this the next day:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434383ra/875997.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <span id="freeText9348583191425268207" style="display:none">OMG !!!!!!!!!! MY HEART CANNOT TAKE THIS!!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />Quinn Loftis is by far my fave author and this series has caused me to lose sleep, cry and fall in love with Decebel. However, I don't know how Quinn keeps topping each book! I was a hot mess for Book 5 and this is no different. Cried my eyes out at this one... <br /><br />But, I shall remain calm while I write this review. Well, I will try anyway.<br /><br />Best part of the book: OMG! From page 1 till the last word of this book was perfection. I am not just saying that because I love Decebel, either. Fate and Fury picks up right where Beyond the Veil ended, the females are trying to get the males back from the In-Between. Let's not forget that Mona, the witch, is still trying to kill them and, adding to that, Lilly (Jacque's mother) is mated! WHAT?!?! Just pure craziness. Now, another thing that I love about Quinn is she never forgets a character. In this book she brings back all kinds of characters and I love that. Now, I know that I am rambling a bit, that is because I don't want to spoil. So, let's make a list:<br /><br />Mona is still trying to kill the pack<br />Males still stuck in the In-between<br />Females are trying to get them back<br />The Great Luna is calling out to all the packs<br />There is going to be a HUGE WAR<br />and Decebel is still the hottest wolf<br />Yep, that sums it up. <br /><br />Not so great about this book: QUINN LOFTIS HOW COULD YOU??!! Quinn needs to change her name to "QUEEN OF THE CLIFFHANGERS". She ripped my heart out throughout this book, but the very last few pages KILLED ME!! I MEAN REALLY KILLED ME!!! I was crying to hard my eyes were puffy the next day. UGH! In my crazy, Book Nerd mind I think she was writing those last few pages with me in mind, trying to figure out if I could survive it.<br /><br />When does book 7 come out??????????????</span>

  <span id="freeText14155024345396503096" style="display:none">May I start off by saying that Quinn Loftis has truly outdone herself yet again on this latest addition to the Grey Wolves Series! It is jam packed with all of the emotions you can think of that carry you through this next stage in the pack’s adventures. It holds you until the end and keeps you craving more!! I was so drawn into the book I could not put it down because I had to know what was going to happen next. Quinn does an amazing job at making you feel like you are right there beside your favorite characters experiencing, hoping, and fighting right along with them! <br /><br />Fate and Furry begins strong and stays that way the entire way through. If you know the series (and you must read them before this book) then start doing a happy dance because this book does not disappoint! Jacque, Jen, Sally, their mates, and friends created along the way continue in their fight for not only their pack’s safety but also the safety of Earth from the twisted Mona. <br /><br />Quinn takes you on a roller coaster ride with new characters, soft moments we love, a little heartbreak, and a whole lot of Quinn Loftis magic…So you better hang on tight because you are going to LOVE this!!</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer938035144" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5498689600060205697">Fate and Fury by Quinn Loftis is book six of the Gray Wolves. Bringing back all our favorite characters, plus a few surprises, this installment really clenches the deal on our hearts, giving them away completely to the Gray Wolves.<br/><br/>PS: spoilers if you haven’t read earlier books in the series!<br/><br/>Joined by Cypher, Lily, Peri, Adam, and Elle, the Romanian and Serbian packs are preparing for war and trying not to open the Veil. The torture of the In-Between threatens to take their mates from them, but t</span>
  <span id="freeText5498689600060205697" style="display:none">Fate and Fury by Quinn Loftis is book six of the Gray Wolves. Bringing back all our favorite characters, plus a few surprises, this installment really clenches the deal on our hearts, giving them away completely to the Gray Wolves.<br /><br />PS: spoilers if you haven’t read earlier books in the series!<br /><br />Joined by Cypher, Lily, Peri, Adam, and Elle, the Romanian and Serbian packs are preparing for war and trying not to open the Veil. The torture of the In-Between threatens to take their mates from them, but the girls are on a rescue mission and they won’t let anything stand between them and their men. Without the men and the alphas that can unit the packs, the wolves won’t stand a chance against Desmonda. Of course, the witch has plans for Sally and Rachel, the two remaining gypsy healers. Peri’s going crazy trying to keep the girls protected while helping them rescue their men. <br />My favorite part about this installment, other than the wild adventure and loyalty, was the strengthening bond between the girls and their guys. The In-Between tests the men to their limits, and the girls have to come in and pick up the pieces. Their relationship is tested, strained, and only continual love gets them through each day.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552142172" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13133111497507457963">******SMALL SPOILERS******Quinn Loftis' highly anticipated Fate & Fury (book 6 TGWS) does not disappoint. Quinn doesn't miss a beat, she immediately plunges the reader deep into the wolves' crumbling world. The sadistic witch Mona is still plotting to destroy all the kind hearted with her evil, as she pulls the weak willed into her devious plan. Meanwhile Jacque, Jen & Sally have come face to face with their darkest fears. They must rely on themselves & their inner strengths to help repair the b</span>
  <span id="freeText13133111497507457963" style="display:none">******SMALL SPOILERS******Quinn Loftis' highly anticipated Fate &amp; Fury (book 6 TGWS) does not disappoint. Quinn doesn't miss a beat, she immediately plunges the reader deep into the wolves' crumbling world. The sadistic witch Mona is still plotting to destroy all the kind hearted with her evil, as she pulls the weak willed into her devious plan. Meanwhile Jacque, Jen &amp; Sally have come face to face with their darkest fears. They must rely on themselves &amp; their inner strengths to help repair the bonds with their mates in order for the pack to fight as a untied front. The wolves however are not alone in this fight. They find allies among unexpected creatures &amp; create a great army to fight against Mona.<br /><br />Leave it to Quinn to sprinkle in laughter in the darkest moments, usually in the form of the ever amusing &amp; sarcastic Jen. My favorite quote. "Walk away from sex on a stick."<br /><br />Quinn's Fate &amp; Furry will take you on an emotional roller coaster in which you'll see your favorite characters pushed to the breaking point, to learn the virtue of reliance &amp; the reward of deep love. <br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560825783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10603408556459751487">The battle with Evil (with a capital E or should I say D for Desdemona) is coming to a head. All the main men have been captured and are being tormented so it’s up to the fabulous babes to set them free. The “Great Luna” is making herself known, calling all the packs, which also involves the Fae. Jacque’s mom is the high warlock Cypher’s mate pulling them into the battle...and Cypher must find a way to follow through with the blood oath or Lily will suffer – which brings in the elves. Yes, they </span>
  <span id="freeText10603408556459751487" style="display:none">The battle with Evil (with a capital E or should I say D for Desdemona) is coming to a head. All the main men have been captured and are being tormented so it’s up to the fabulous babes to set them free. The “Great Luna” is making herself known, calling all the packs, which also involves the Fae. Jacque’s mom is the high warlock Cypher’s mate pulling them into the battle...and Cypher must find a way to follow through with the blood oath or Lily will suffer – which brings in the elves. Yes, they are all here! <br /><br />Wow, what an incredible story! Quinn Loftis's vivid and in your face writing style pulls you right into this fabulous story. As with all her books, the witty banter between the characters is the perfect icing on the cake! <br /><br />The ending, ouch! It was like a physical blow. Decebel what the heck!!! Of course it left us wanting more. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10603408556459751487" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/553615499" />
    <a title="QueenMommy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18105119-queenmommy"><img alt="QueenMommy" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/553615499?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="QueenMommy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="QueenMommy" href="/user/show/18105119-queenmommy">QueenMommy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18105119-queenmommy?shelf=ya-paranormal">ya-paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553615499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12633228363839332534">I wish I was as good with words as the awesome authors I choose to read but I can share how I felt during and after reading Fate and Fury. I was giddy, excited, anxious, shocked, happy, captivated, sad, eager, and ecstatic. But one feeling I was NOT, was disappointed. Quinn has done it again with Fate and Fury, she has managed to continue an awesome journey for all of our beloved characters as well as introduce us to some new characters, so get ready!<br/><br/>One of the many reasons I love Quinn's books </span>
  <span id="freeText12633228363839332534" style="display:none">I wish I was as good with words as the awesome authors I choose to read but I can share how I felt during and after reading Fate and Fury. I was giddy, excited, anxious, shocked, happy, captivated, sad, eager, and ecstatic. But one feeling I was NOT, was disappointed. Quinn has done it again with Fate and Fury, she has managed to continue an awesome journey for all of our beloved characters as well as introduce us to some new characters, so get ready!<br /><br />One of the many reasons I love Quinn's books is how she continues to develop her characters and keep them just as active in her stories . Unlike so many authors who have written series the past characters melt into the background but that is NOT so in Quinn's books! For those of us who have fallen in love with Fane/Jacque, Dec/Jen, and Costin/Sally, get excited because they are all in this book and each get time in the spotlight. Thank you, thank you Quinn for giving this gift to your readers. We fall in love with them ALL and WANT to see what is happening in their lives and Quinn delivers that!<br /><br />Another HUGE reason I LOVE Quinn's books is how she describes and develops the love of the mates! It is unlike any other books I've read and so sweet! You can't help but fall in love with these mates. Who doesn't want to be loved like that? What am I talking about or how does Quinn make that different than another author, go read her books and find out!!! <br /><br />These days time is so precious and so we may be selective on who or what we read not wanting to waste our time. I promise you that if you allow Quinn's books a chance, it will be worth your time, in fact you will lose track of time. I know that I did! <br /><br />Get ready to join Quinn in is this awesome story and dive in with the Pack as they battle it out with Mona the witch. It was a nail biter and action packed the WHOLE time, I'm not kidding! Yes and definitely more Costin and Sally time (sigh)! I just love them. I agree with other reviews that this book is probably the darkest book so far but not in a bad way, in a way that shows the maturity of the girls, the seriousness of the battle and the love and even struggle of the mates!<br /><br />As always I will be begging Quinn to continue to write more GWS books and look forward to the next one. Wow, that sounds so passive, "look forward to", more like DYING to get my hands on the next book, HOW WILL I LIVE until the next book! :Yep, Quinn's books are that good!!!!! We may need to start a support group for her fans. :)<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12633228363839332534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_557641931" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/557641931" />
    <a title="Naomi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7602600-naomi"><img alt="Naomi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328234890p2/7602600.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/557641931?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Naomi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Naomi" href="/user/show/7602600-naomi">Naomi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7602600-naomi?shelf=ya-paranormal">ya-paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer557641931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12492408097122028968">ARC Review<br/>Grey Wolves fans, get ready! All your favorite characters are back and ready to kick a witch's butt. Quinn listened to you, fans! She adores you and it shows in this book. The three original friends and their mates are back, front and center. Hope you love that as much as I did. <br/><br/>Because this is an ARC review of the sixth (but not last) book in a series, I have to admit to some prejudices about the characters before giving my comments. <br/>1. I LOVE Adam. I think he's my favorite character </span>
  <span id="freeText12492408097122028968" style="display:none">ARC Review<br />Grey Wolves fans, get ready! All your favorite characters are back and ready to kick a witch's butt. Quinn listened to you, fans! She adores you and it shows in this book. The three original friends and their mates are back, front and center. Hope you love that as much as I did. <br /><br />Because this is an ARC review of the sixth (but not last) book in a series, I have to admit to some prejudices about the characters before giving my comments. <br />1. I LOVE Adam. I think he's my favorite character overall not just guy-wise, although Costin and Fane are close 2nds, guy-wise.<br />2. I relate more to Sally and Jacque than Jen (never been the smartass bombshell, so sometimes I just don't like the sarcasm).<br />3. I am a sappy love nerd.<br /><br />Quinn's writing has always captured my heart, and the sixth installment of this series started out amazing. Throughout the book there were lots of ups and downs, answered questions and new mysteries, old characters, new characters, and that tender, heart-melting and heart-wrenching thing called LOVE. <br /><br />This book tells us more about Costin and Sally, giving them their moment, but Quinn didn't forget about everyone else. We see the strength of certain characters *ahem, Vasile* that we've been hearing about as well as the next moments in the lives of Jacque &amp; Fane, Jen &amp; Dec, Adam &amp; Crina, Sorin &amp; Elle, Cypher and Lilly, Dillon and his mate, Cyn and ..., shh! Also, quite a bit more from Vasile &amp; Alina. Mona is back, and I really enjoyed her perspective. Plus, new characters I can't wait to find out more about. Oh, and Costin? Um, yes, please! Wait til he shows you what he can do.<br /><br />With so many characters and mini-plots, there were times when I got distracted from the main plot line, but I always felt like I was getting need-to-know info. I wish Sally and Costin had more dedicated time to them and that the new pairs from BTV also got a bit more length to their stories (perhaps in book 7?). But with dominant males everywhere, Mona's nasty tricks, and some serious end of the world pressure, no wonder everyone was working their tails off to find a way to save the world. <br /><br />Like Candace said, this book is edgier than the others. IMHO, it has moved beyond YA while still clean. There are some dark moments that mirror the sometimes harsh reality of real life, but the bonds, friendship and love that attracted us to Quinn's characters in the first place grow stronger as the individuals that compose them endure. This ain't no happily ever after, everything is hunky-dory book. These couples are full of LIFE and they are learning what it means to have a mate, forever.<br /><br />I think you are going to love this book. And the ending? Yeah, it's SO good and so Grey Wolves (aka it's gonna punch you in the stomach).<br /><br />Go get it, now! <br /><br />Thanks for reading this review,<br />Naomi</span>
  <a data-text-id="12492408097122028968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_559044353" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559044353" />
    <a title="Sheri" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7300331-sheri"><img alt="Sheri" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378517294p2/7300331.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559044353?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sheri" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sheri" href="/user/show/7300331-sheri">Sheri</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559044353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9626342469395130364"><b>Fiercely Fur-tastic. Substantial sarcasm. Jaw-dropping conclusion. </b><br/><br/>I must say, the grey wolves have held a special place in my kindle for quite some time. <br/>Book six? Really? <br/>Wow!! That’s hard to believe. <br/>The gang is still as tight as ever, as well as sidesplitting hysterical. It kicks off with the men trapped in the in-between and their women are determined to save them. For some reason, this was hard for me to get into. I struggled with some of the new faces and mixed up names with who was who m</span>
  <span id="freeText9626342469395130364" style="display:none"><b>Fiercely Fur-tastic. Substantial sarcasm. Jaw-dropping conclusion. </b><br /><br />I must say, the grey wolves have held a special place in my kindle for quite some time. <br />Book six? Really? <br />Wow!! That’s hard to believe. <br />The gang is still as tight as ever, as well as sidesplitting hysterical. It kicks off with the men trapped in the in-between and their women are determined to save them. For some reason, this was hard for me to get into. I struggled with some of the new faces and mixed up names with who was who more than once.<br /><br />Jacque’s mom Lilly, is fun and funny, and I enjoyed watching her new-found happiness bloom. I have always loved the humor the girls have and they have a gift; for they can crack a smile on my face in an instant.<br /> Yet, it seemed like all the ladies drank the Jen Kool-Aid and the sarcasm was sooo thick at times it was distracting. Everyone including Lilly had a smart mouth and unfortunately, I found it took away from the original three <i>smart ass</i> musketeer’s. The warlock king has won my heart and I was biting my fingernails when ‘his plan’ was in the works.<br /> <br />Several heart stopping moments took my breath away, especially Decebel's final scene. <br />Oh, my sweet gruff stubborn Dec. I am praying to the fates that he slips into a loophole and finds a way out of his promise. For all the grey wolves’ sanity, there must be a way to stop what ‘must be’ and create a new future.<br /><br />Sluggish in the beginning…<br />lightning fast second half…<br />with an intense, unbelievable and action-packed conclusion.<br /><br />I was wide awake and salivating for more as the last pages flew by and can guarantee I will snatch up the next and final book for one more ride with these lovely furry friends.<br /><br /><b>*4.5 <i>escalating &amp; extreme </i>stars*</b> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9626342469395130364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ibAkxYT0MBI0bk7/Xz8xreU/B/hHz3FQM/Upx5mvMkj5BMf1W+/8YuvafombJNnxb8Bf02LBNGWmQBNdfymNjg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/geP6M2V6y34b11GA43l5p1lHQRQcs1Wn2dVgwOX2oCOs2zYEo4nXSfbbTDHlg26F5pFL3V8iGMK0m8Z5RFlRg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7419692773760853088">Hello, Readers. My name is Quinn Loftis and I am lucky enough to call myself a novelist. In 2011, I self-published my first novel, Prince of Wolves with no expectations, other than my friends and family might purchase the book out of pity. Now, several years later, with 30+ novels and counting under my belt, Prince of Wolves had been downloaded over 1 million times. Though I was hesitant at the ti</span>
  <span id="freeText7419692773760853088" style="display:none">Hello, Readers. My name is Quinn Loftis and I am lucky enough to call myself a novelist. In 2011, I self-published my first novel, Prince of Wolves with no expectations, other than my friends and family might purchase the book out of pity. Now, several years later, with 30+ novels and counting under my belt, Prince of Wolves had been downloaded over 1 million times. Though I was hesitant at the time to submit my work to the world for their scrutiny, I'm so glad I did. It made my dream of making a living by telling stories a reality. <br /><br />I'm blessed to share my household my wonderful husband of more than twenty years (who also co-writes with me on occasion), three beautiful sons, a French Bulldog, and an oversized tabby cat. I love hearing from readers, so if you have any questions about the books or my journey, don't hesitate to hit the 'Contact Quinn' in the menu above. Thank you so much for taking a chance on my books.</span>

Yet, every time evil thinks it’s gotten the upper hand, the wolves come roaring back to protect their own. No darkness can stand against them, especially when they fight united with their supernatural allies. But what happens when the darkness refuses to stand and fight? Instead, it flees, spreading across an entire continent, infecting the supernatural races as it goes. Will the wolves be able to stand against the hidden darkness, the Order of the Burning Claw, or will they crumble as it shakes them to their foundations? Sally, the group’s gypsy healer, is home with her pack, seemingly recovered from the psychic assault against her mind. Unbeknownst to the pack and its leaders, however, something sinister has followed in her wake. Vasile and his wolves will need the help of Thalion, prince of the elves, if they are to find a way to fight the veiled evil threatening both human and supernatural alike. But Thalion has his own mysteries to unravel. His father, Ludcarab, the elven king, is discovered alive, after having been lost for centuries.
